132→func DiagnosticPlainFromJSON(diag *viewsjson.Diagnostic, width int) string {\n   133→\tif diag == nil {\n   134→\t\t// No good reason to pass a nil diagnostic in here...\n   135→\t\treturn \"\"\n snippet.FunctionCall; callInfo != nil && callInfo.Signature != nil {\n   298→\n   299→\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(buf, color.Color(\"    [dark_gray]│[reset] while calling [bold]%s[reset](\"), callInfo.CalledAs)\n   300→\t\t\t\tfor i, param := range callInfo.Signature.Params {\n   301→\t\t\t\t\tif i > 0 {\n   302→\t\t\t\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\", \")\n   303→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   304→\t\t\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(param.Name)\n   305→\t\t\t\t}\n   306→\t\t\t\tif param := callInfo.Signature.VariadicParam; param != nil {\n   307→\t\t\t\t\tif len(callInfo.Signature.Params) > 0 {\n   308→\t\t\t\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\", \")\n   309→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   310→\t\t\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(param.Name)\n   311→\t\t\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"...\")\n   312→\t\t\t\t}\n   313→\t\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\")\\n\")\n   314→\t\t\t}\n   315→\t\t\tfor _, value := range values {\n   316→\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(buf, color.Color(\"    [dark_gray]│[reset] [bold]%s[reset] %s\\n\"), value.Traversal, value.Statement)\n   317→\t\t\t}\n   318→\t\t}\n   319→\t}\n   320→\n   321→\tbuf.WriteByte('\\n')\n   322→}\n   323→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should If set to zero, messages will not be wrapped by this function\n// at all. Although the long-form text parts of the message are wrapped,\n// not all aspects of the message are guaranteed to fit within the specified\n// terminal width.\nfunc Diagnostic(diag tfdiags.Diagnostic, sources map[string][]byte, color *colorstring.Colorize, width int) string {\n\treturn DiagnosticFromJSON(viewsjson.NewDiagnostic(diag, sources), color, width)\n}\n\nfunc DiagnosticFromJSON(diag *viewsjson.Diagnostic, color *colorstring.Colorize, width int) string {\n\tif diag == nil {\n\t\t// No good reason to pass a nil diagnostic in here...\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// these leftRule* variables are markers for the beginning of the lines\n\t// containing the diagnostic that are intended to help sighted users\n\t// better understand the information hierarchy when diagnostics appear\n\t// alongside other information or alongside other diagnostics.\n\t//\n\t// Without this, it seems (based on folks sharing incomplete messages when\n\t// asking questions, or including extra content that's not part of the\n\t// diagnostic) that some readers have trouble easily identifying which\n\t// text belongs to the diagnostic and which does not.\n\tvar leftRuleLine, leftRuleStart, leftRuleEnd string\n\tvar leftRuleWidth int // in visual character cells\n\n\tswitch diag.Severity {\n\tcase viewsjson.DiagnosticSeverityError:\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(color.Color(\"[bold][red]Error: [reset]\"))\n\t\tleftRuleLine = color.Color(\"[red]│[reset] \")\n\t\tleftRuleStart = color.Color(\"[red]╷[reset]\")\n\t\tleftRuleEnd = color.Color(\"[red]╵[reset]\")\n\t\tleftRuleWidth = 2\n\tcase viewsjson.DiagnosticSeverityWarning:\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(color.Color(\"[bold][yellow]Warning: [reset]\"))\n\t\tleftRuleLine = color.Color(\"[yellow]│[reset] \")\n\t\tleftRuleStart = color.Color(\"[yellow]╷[reset]\")\n\t\tleftRuleEnd = color.Color(\"[yellow]╵[reset]\")\n\t\tleftRuleWidth = 2\n\tdefault:\n\t\t// Clear out any coloring that might be applied by Terraform's UI helper,\n\t\t// so our result is not context-sensitive.\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(color.Color(\"\\n[reset]\"))\n\t}\n\n\t// We don't wrap the summary, since we expect it to be terse, and since\n\t// this is where we put the text of a native Go error it may not always\n\t// be pure text that lends itself well to word-wrapping.\n\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, color.Color(\"[bold]%s[reset]\\n\\n\"), diag.Summary)\n\n\tappendSourceSnippets(&buf, diag, color)\n\n\tif diag.Detail != \"\" {\n\t\tparaWidth := width - leftRuleWidth - 1 // leave room for the left rule\n\t\tif paraWidth > 0 {\n\t\t\tlines := strings.Split(diag.Detail, \"\\n\")\n\t\t\tfor _, line := range lines {\n\t\t\t\tif !strings.HasPrefix(line, \" \") {\n\t\t\t\t\tline = wordwrap.WrapString(line, uint(paraWidth))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"%s\\n\", line)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"%s\\n\", diag.Detail)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Before we return, we'll finally add the left rule prefixes to each\n\t// line so that the overall message is visually delimited from what's\n\t// around it. We'll do that by scanning over what we already generated\n\t// and adding the prefix for each line.\n\tvar ruleBuf strings.Builder\n\tsc := bufio.NewScanner(&buf)\n\truleBuf.WriteString(leftRuleStart)\n\truleBuf.WriteByte('\\n')\n\tfor sc.Scan() {\n\t\tline := sc.Text()\n\t\tprefix := leftRuleLine\n\t\tif line == \"\" {\n\t\t\t// Don't print the space after the line if there would be nothing\n\t\t\t// after it anyway.\n\t\t\tprefix = strings.TrimSpace(prefix)\n\t\t}\n\t\truleBuf.WriteString(prefix)\n\t\truleBuf.WriteString(line)\n\t\truleBuf.WriteByte('\\n')\n\t}\n\truleBuf.WriteString(leftRuleEnd)\n\truleBuf.WriteByte('\\n')\n\n\treturn ruleBuf.String()\n}\n\n// DiagnosticPlain is an alternative to Diagnostic which minimises the use of\n// virtual terminal formatting sequences.\n//\n// It is intended for use in automation and other contexts in which diagnostic\n// messages are parsed from the Terraform output.\nfunc DiagnosticPlain(diag tfdiags.Diagnostic, sources map[string][]byte, width int) string {\n\treturn DiagnosticPlainFromJSON(viewsjson.NewDiagnostic(diag, sources), width)\n}\n\nfunc DiagnosticPlainFromJSON(diag *viewsjson.Diagnostic, width int) string {\n\tif diag == nil {\n\t\t// No good reason to pass a nil diagnostic in here...\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\tswitch diag.Severity {\n\tcase viewsjson.DiagnosticSeverityError:\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\nError: \")\n\tcase viewsjson.DiagnosticSeverityWarning:\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\nWarning: \")\n\tdefault:\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// We don't wrap the summary, since we expect it to be terse, and {\n\t\t\t\t\tb.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\"  on %s line %d\\n\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmainSource.Subject.Filename,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmainSource.Subject.Start.Line,\n\t\t\t\t\t))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t} b.String()\n}\n\nfunc appendSourceSnippets(buf *bytes.Buffer, diag *viewsjson.Diagnostic, color *colorstring.Colorize) {\n\tif diag.Address != \"\" {\n\t\tfmt.Fprintf(buf, \"  with %s,\\n\", diag.Address)\n\t}\n\n\tif diag.Range == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tif diag.Snippet == nil {\n\t\t// This should generally not happen, as long as sources are always\n\t\t// loaded through the main snippet and render the highlighted section with underlines\n\t\tstart := snippet.HighlightStartOffset\n\t\tend := snippet.HighlightEndOffset\n\n\t\t// Only buggy diagnostics can have an end range before the start, but\n\t\t// we need to ensure we don't crash here if that happens.\n\t\tif end < start {\n\t\t\tend = start + 1\n\t\t\tif end > len(code) {\n\t\t\t\tend = if there's a bug in the code generating\n\t\t// the snippet objects.\n\t\tif start < 0 {\n\t\t\tstart = 0\n\t\t} else if start > len(code) {\n\t\t\tstart = len(code)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif end < 0 {\n\t\t\tend = 0\n\t\t} else if end > len(code) {\n\t\t\tend = len(code)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbefore, highlight, after := code[0:start], code[start:end], code[end:]\n\t\tcode = && snippet.FunctionCall.Signature != nil) {\n\t\t\t// The diagnostic may also have information about the dynamic\n\t\t\t// values of relevant variables at the point of evaluation.\n\t\t\t// This is particularly useful for expressions that get evaluated\n\t\t\t// multiple times with different values, such as blocks using\n\t\t\t// \"count\" and \"for_each\", or within \"for\" expressions.\n\t\t\tvalues := make([]viewsjson.DiagnosticExpressionValue, len(snippet.Values))\n\t\t\tcopy(values, snippet.Values)\n\t\t\tsort.Slice(values, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\t\treturn 65→\t\t}\n    66→\n    67→\t\trcs, err := rc.Encode(schema.Block.ImpliedType())\n    68→\t\tif err != nil {\n    69→\t\t\treturn changesSrc, fmt.Errorf(\"Changes.Encode: %w\", err)\n    70→\t\t}\n Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.\n// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1\n\npackage format\n\nimport (\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output,\n// showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format produces a compact diff summary of the given plan.\n// It outputs one line per resource change grouped by action type and\n// includes summary counts at the end.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action type\n\tchanges := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed resources\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Skip no-op changes\n\t\tif rc.Action == plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tchanges[rc.Action] = append(changes[rc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order of action types to display\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Renew,\n\t\tplans.Open,\n\t\tplans.Close,\n\t}\n\n\tvar result strings.Builder\n\n\t// Count totals for summary\n\ttotalCount := len(plan.Changes.Resources)\n\tactionCounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\n\t// Process changes in defined order\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tresources, exists := changes[action]\n\t\tif !exists || len(resources) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action group header\n\t\tactionSymbol := DiffActionSymbol(action)\n\t\tactionName := formatActionName(action)\n\t\tresult.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"\\n%s %s:\\n\", actionSymbol, actionName))\n\n\t\t// Write each resource in this group\n\t\tfor _, rc := range resources {\n\t\t\tresult.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", rc.Addr.String()))\n\t\t\tactionCounts[action]++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary\n\tif len(plan.Changes.Resources) > 0 {\n\t\tresult.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t\tresult.WriteString(formatSummary(actionCounts))\n\t}\n\n\treturn result.String()\n}\n\n// formatActionName returns a human-readable name for an action.\nfunc formatActionName(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"Create\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"Read\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"Update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"Delete\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"Replace (delete then create)\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"Replace (create then delete)\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.Renew:\n\t\treturn \"Renew\"\n\tcase plans.Open:\n\t\treturn \"Open\"\n\tcase plans.Close:\n\t\treturn \"Close\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// formatSummary produces a summary line showing counts by action type.\nfunc formatSummary(counts map[plans.Action]int) string {\n\tvar parts []string\n\n\t// Build summary in a consistent order\n\tsummaryOrder := []struct CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output,\n// showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format produces a compact diff summary of the given plan.\n// It outputs one line per resource change grouped by action type and\n// includes summary counts at the end.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action type\n\tchanges := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed resources\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Skip no-op changes\n\t\tif rc.Action == plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tchanges[rc.Action] = append(changes[rc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order of action types to display\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Renew,\n\t\tplans.Open,\n\t\tplans.Close,\n\t}\n\n\tvar result strings.Builder\n\n\t// Count totals for summary\n\ttotalCount := len(plan.Changes.Resources)\n\tactionCounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\n\t// Process changes in defined order\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tresources, exists := changes[action]\n\t\tif !exists || len(resources) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action group header\n\t\tactionSymbol := DiffActionSymbol(action)\n\t\tactionName := formatActionName(action)\n\t\tresult.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"\\n%s %s:\\n\", actionSymbol, actionName))\n\n\t\t// Write each resource in this group\n\t\tfor _, rc := range resources {\n\t\t\tresult.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", rc.Addr.String()))\n\t\t\tactionCounts[action]++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary\n\tif len(plan.Changes.Resources) > 0 {\n\t\tresult.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t\tresult.WriteString(formatSummary(actionCounts))\n\t}\n\n\treturn result.String()\n}\n\n// formatActionName returns a human-readable name for an action.\nfunc formatActionName(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"Create\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"Read\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"Update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"Delete\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"Replace (delete then create)\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"Replace (create then delete)\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.Renew:\n\t\treturn \"Renew\"\n\tcase plans.Open:\n\t\treturn \"Open\"\n\tcase plans.Close:\n\t\treturn \"Close\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// formatSummary produces a summary line showing counts by action type.\nfunc formatSummary(counts map[plans.Action]int) string {\n\tvar parts []string\n\n\t// Build summary in a consistent order\n\tsummaryOrder := []struct {\n\t\taction plans.Action\n\t\tlabel  string\n\t}{\n\t\t{plans.Create, \"add\"},\n\t\t{plans.Update, \"change\"},\n\t\t{plans.Delete, \"destroy\"},\n\t\t{plans.DeleteThenCreate, \"replace\"},\n\t\t{plans.CreateThenDelete, \"replace\"},\n\t\t{plans.CreateThenForget, \"forget\"},\n\t\t{plans.Forget, \"forget\"},\n\t\t{plans.Read, \"read\"},\n\t\t{plans.Renew, \"renew\"},\n\t\t{plans.Open, \"open\"},\n\t\t{plans.Close, \"close\"},\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, item := range summaryOrder {\n\t\tif count, exists := counts[item.action]; exists && count > 0 {\n\t\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to %s\", count, item.label))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"No changes.\"\n\t}\n\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Plan: %s.\\n\", strings.Join(parts, \", 25→\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n    26→\t\treturn \"\"\n    27→\t}\n    28→\n    29→\t// Group changes by action type\n    30→\tchanges := a compact diff summary of the given plan.\n// It outputs one line per resource change grouped by action type and\n// includes summary counts at the end.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan result strings.Builder\n\n\t// Count totals for summary\n\tactionCounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\n\t// Process changes in defined order\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tresources, exists := changes[action]\n\t\tif !exists || len(resources) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action group header\n\t\tactionSymbol := DiffActionSymbol(action)\n\t\tactionName :=
